On resume, the code attempts to re-enable it if `chip->msi` is set, but if `pci_enable_msi` fails, it just clears the flag without properly handling the error state or the implications for the device's interrupt handling.\n\nThe real issue seems to be that codec communication times out after suspend/resume. Looking at the error pattern: the driver works fine initially, but after a suspend/resume cycle, `azx_get_response` starts timing out. Once that happens, it falls back to single_cmd mode.
